<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究致密天体阴影中尖点形成的普遍规律，探索独立于具体时空度规的普适特征，为未来黑洞观测中识别非克尔特征提供模型无关的框架。

Method: 系统分析具有运行牛顿耦合的克尔黑洞阴影，将框架扩展到旋转可穿越虫洞，研究尖点形成伴随的拓扑电荷跃迁、等面积定律和临界标度行为。

Result: 发现尖点形成伴随三种相互关联的普适现象：拓扑电荷跃迁、自相交结构的等面积定律和临界标度行为，这些特征在克尔黑洞和旋转可穿越虫洞中都存在，独立于具体度规细节。

Conclusion: 揭示了致密天体阴影中尖点形成的普适性，为未来黑洞观测中识别非克尔特征提供了模型无关的理论框架，表明这些现象源于阴影的全局形态而非具体度规细节。

Abstract: This work investigates the universality of cusp formation in the shadows of compact objects. We demonstrate that, because these phenomena originate from the global morphology of the shadow, they are fundamentally independent of specific spacetime metric details and apply across diverse models. These features are systematically analyzed for the Kerr black hole endowed with a running Newton coupling. By extending our framework to rotating traversable wormholes, we confirm that the same universal behavior persists in more general compact objects. Our study uncovers the universality underlying cusp formation, offering a model-independent framework for identifying non-Kerr signatures in future black hole observations.

</details>


### [131] [Microstate Counting for rotating (type~II) isolated horizons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19763)
*Pritam Nanda*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 提出一种在圈量子引力中计算旋转黑洞微观状态的方法，通过将视界分解为同心环，每个环近似为局部非旋转区域，从而恢复局部Chern-Simons描述并包含角动量贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准非旋转黑洞熵推导无法直接扩展到旋转孤立视界，因为旋转1形式破坏了视界上的全局Chern-Simons结构。需要克服这一障碍来包含角动量贡献。

Method: 将视界S^2局部分解为窄同心环，每个环近似为局部非旋转区域，具有恒定有效CS能级。每个环使用标准LQG技术独立量子化，总熵通过对整个视界积分获得。

Result: 该方法恢复了局部CS描述，包含了角动量贡献，且与黑洞力学第一定律一致，为旋转黑洞提供了微观状态计数方案。

Conclusion: 提出的局部分解方法成功解决了旋转黑洞在圈量子引力中的微观状态计数问题，将标准非旋转熵推导扩展到包含角动量的情况。

Abstract: We present a proposal for black hole microstate counting in Loop Quantum Gravity (LQG) for rotating (type~II) isolated horizons. The key obstacle in extending the standard nonrotating entropy derivation arises from the $θ$-dependent rotation 1-form, which breaks the global Chern--Simons (CS) structure on the horizon. We propose a local decomposition of the horizon $S^2$ into narrow concentric rings, each approximated as a locally nonrotating patch with a constant effective CS level. Each ring is quantized independently using standard LQG techniques, and the total entropy is obtained by integrating over the entire horizon. This method restores a local CS description, includes the contribution of angular momentum, and is consistent with the first law of black hole mechanics.

### [132] [Chaotic motion and power spectral density in Schwarzschild Bertotti-Robinson black hole spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19797)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究黑洞周围磁场对粒子动力学的影响，特别是Schwarzschild-BR黑洞在弱场极限下退化为浸入均匀磁场中的Schwarzschild黑洞的情况，探索磁场参数如何影响粒子轨道稳定性和运动特性。

Conclusion: Schwarzschild-BR黑洞周围的磁场对粒子动力学有重要影响，磁场参数的增加会扩大稳定轨道区域，磁场、电荷和磁矩的相互作用导致复杂的动力学行为，包括混沌现象。

Abstract: In this paper, we show that in weak field limit Schwarzschild Bertotti-Robinson black hole (Schwarzschild-BR BH) turns into Schwarzschild black hole immersed in external uniform magnetic field which is given in 1. The dynamics of both magnetized and electrically charged particles in the vicinity of a Schwarzschild-BR black hole are investigated. The innermost stable circular orbits (ISCOs) for both magnetized and electrically charged particles are examined in detail, revealing that the magnetic field parameter B exerts a considerable influence, leading to an increase in the ISCO radius. The orbital and epicyclic motion of test particles in Schwarzschild-BR black hole spacetime was analyzed, including both circular orbits and their oscillatory perturbations. Additionally, the trajectories of both magnetized and electrically charged particles are analyzed for various configurations of the magnetic parameter B. We also demonstrate how the magnetic field B, electric charge q, and magnetic moment μ influence the dynamics of charged particles, specifically affecting the chaotic behavior, Poincare' sections, oscillatory frequencies and power spectral density.

### [133] [Casimir-Induced Quintessence in Dark Dimension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19819)
*Tomoki Katayama,Hiroki Matsui,Yuri Michinobu,Fumiya Okamatsu,Yutaka Sakamura,Takahiro Terada*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 在暗维度框架中，通过大额外维度的卡西米尔能量解释暗能量，引入额外自由度使radion场作为quintessence场缓慢演化，与DESI观测一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索暗维度场景的具体实现，其中亚毫米尺度的大额外维度中，体场的卡西米尔能量可以解释观测到的暗能量现象。

Method: 在5维设置中，标准模型限制在4维膜上，推导radion的有效作用量。考虑仅含引力和三个右手体态中微子的最小模型，并扩展包含额外体自由度以产生平坦的正势能。

Result: 最小模型通常产生负的radion势能；通过引入额外体自由度，可以产生足够平坦的正势能，使radion作为quintessence场在亚电子伏特尺度缓慢演化，与DESI BAO测量一致。

Conclusion: 暗维度框架可以通过适当选择体自由度实现正的真空能量，使radion场作为quintessence场解释暗能量，与当前观测数据兼容。

Abstract: We investigate a concrete realization of the Dark Dimension scenario, where a single large extra dimension is set at sub-millimeter scales. In this framework, the Casimir energy of bulk fields accounts for the observed dark energy. Working in a 5-dimensional setup with the Standard Model confined to a 4-dimensional brane, we derive the effective action for the radion. We demonstrate that a minimal model comprising only gravity and three right-handed bulk neutrinos typically yields a negative radion potential. To realize a positive vacuum energy, we consider some extensions with additional bulk degrees of freedom. These extensions generate a sufficiently flat positive potential that allows the radion to behave as a quintessence field, evolving slowly at the sub-eV scale. Finally, we analyze the evolution of the dark-energy equation-of-state parameter and show that our model is consistent with recent DESI BAO measurements, including the distance ratios $D_H/r_d$ and $D_M/r_d$.

### [134] [Modeling the merger-ringdown of an eccentric test-mass inspiral into a Kerr black hole using the effective-one-body framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19913)
*Guglielmo Faggioli,Alessandra Buonanno,Maarten van de Meent,Gaurav Khanna*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究对克尔黑洞中偏心轨道小质量天体合并-铃坠阶段的引力波进行建模，分析了自旋、偏心率和相对论异常对波形特征的影响，为SEOBNR家族模型提供了测试质量极限下的合并-铃坠模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究偏心自旋对齐双黑洞在接近合并时的引力波特征，特别是残余偏心率对合并-铃坠阶段的影响，为现有有效单体模型提供改进基础。

Method: 使用时域Teukolsky方程代码，结合有效单体框架计算的轨迹，生成克尔黑洞中偏心轨道小质量天体合并-铃坠的引力波形。参数范围包括自旋a∈[-0.9,0.9]、LSO偏心率e_LSO∈[0,0.9]、相对论异常ξ_LSO∈[0,2π]，分析多个球谐模式。

Result: 偏心率主要影响波形最后一个峰值特征，对铃坠信号影响较小；相对论异常仅在参数空间有限部分影响最后一个峰值的形态，对铃坠部分无影响。建立了SEOBNR-TMLE模型的合并-铃坠模型，考虑了铃坠阶段的准正则模式混合。

Conclusion: 该研究为自旋对齐有效单体双黑洞模型的合并-铃坠部分提供了考虑残余偏心率影响的初步模型，可扩展到可比质量情况，是改进现有引力波模型的重要一步。

Abstract: We characterize and phenomenologically model the merger-ringdown of gravitational waves emitted by a small compact object that plunges and merges into a Kerr black hole from equatorial-eccentric inspirals. The waveforms are generated employing a time-domain Teukolsky code sourced with trajectories computed using the effective-one-body framework. We span values of the Kerr spin $a\in[-0.9, 0.9] $, eccentricity at the last stable orbit (LSO) $ e_{\rm LSO} \in [0,0.9] $, and relativistic anomaly $ ξ_{\rm LSO} \in [0 , 2 π]$. We characterize the last peak of the waveform and ringdown features across the parameter space, finding that the eccentricity mainly affects the last peak features, while it has a smaller impact on the ringdown signal. In contrast, the relativistic anomaly measured at the LSO influences the morphology of the last peak in a restricted portion of the parameter space and has no impact on the ringdown part. We perform the analysis for all the spin-weighted spherical harmonic modes normally included in the \texttt{SEOBNR} family of models, $(\ell,m)\in\{ (2,2), (3,3), (4,4), (5,5), (2,1), (3,2), (4,3)\}$. Finally, we introduce a merger-ringdown model for \texttt{SEOB-TMLE}, a forthcoming inspiral-merger-ringdown waveform model for eccentric spin-aligned binary black holes in the test-mass limit, whose features can be extended to comparable-mass regimes. The model also accounts for quasinormal mode mixing during the ringdown. It provides a first step toward incorporating the impact of residual eccentricity close to merger into spin-aligned effective-one-body merger-ringdown models for binary black holes.

### [135] [Analytical Solution of Spinning, Eccentric Binary Black Hole Dynamics at the Second Post-Newtonian Order](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20031)
*Tom Colin,Sashwat Tanay,Laura Bernard*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 开发了2PN精度的解析解，用于模拟具有任意自旋和偏心率的双黑洞系统，相比之前的1.5PN解有数量级改进


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 最近引力波探测显示偏心率和自旋进动特征，需要同时建模具有这些特征的双黑洞系统。现有方法多基于启发式扭曲非进动波形，缺乏第一性原理基础。

Method: 基于广义相对论和后牛顿近似，在已有1.5PN解基础上，构建了2PN阶的解析解，描述相对分离矢量、黑洞自旋矢量和轨道角动量矢量的时间演化。

Result: 新2PN解相比早期1.5PN解有数量级改进，尽管自旋解中的微小轨道时间尺度涨落仅达到1.5PN精度而非2PN，但被忽略的次主导阶振荡影响较小。

Conclusion: 该工作为同时具有自旋和偏心率的双黑洞系统提供了基于第一性原理的引力波建模框架，是向更高精度波形建模的重要进展。

Abstract: Recent gravitational wave (GW) detections showing signatures of eccentricity and spin precession underscore the need to model binary black holes (BBHs) possessing these features simultaneously. Most efforts over the past fifteen years to model spinning BBHs and their corresponding GWs have relied on heuristically twisting waveforms from non-precessing systems. This approach is based on empirical observations rather than first principles. This article aims to model the GWs from spinning and eccentric BBHs from a first-principles approach within general relativity and post-Newtonian (PN) approximation. Building on the already-existing 1.5 PN solution, we construct an analytical solution for the time evolution of the relative separation vector, the individual black hole spin vectors, and the orbital angular momentum vector at 2PN order for BBHs with arbitrary spins and eccentricity. Such a solution is not fully 2PN accurate in that the tiny orbital timescale fluctuations in the solutions for the spins are only leading 1.5PN order accurate, instead of 2PN. However, it is shown that our new 2PN solution is still an order of magnitude improvement over the earlier 1.5PN solution, underlining the sub-dominant nature of the neglected next-to-leading-order oscillations in the spin solutions.

### [136] [Angular momentum tail contributions to compact binary dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20096)
*Gabriel Luz Almeida,Alan Müller,Stefano Foffa,Riccardo Sturani*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 论文推导了致密双星系统中引力辐射通过角动量散射再吸收过程的动力学有效作用量，重点研究了角动量失败尾过程对第六阶后牛顿阶的贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究引力辐射在双星系统中被角动量散射后再吸收的过程，这些角动量失败尾过程对双星系统动力学有重要贡献，特别是在高精度后牛顿展开中。

Method: 推导了包含任意质量和电流多极矩的角动量失败尾过程的动力学有效作用量，特别计算了涉及质量八极矩和电流八极矩（与相反宇称的四极矩混合）对第六阶后牛顿阶的贡献。

Result: 得到了角动量失败尾过程的通用有效作用量表达式，并明确给出了第六阶后牛顿阶的具体贡献项。同时推导了与任意角动量失败尾过程相关的辐射多极矩。

Conclusion: 角动量失败尾过程对致密双星系统动力学有重要贡献，特别是在高精度后牛顿展开中，这些结果对于理解引力辐射散射效应和精确计算双星演化至关重要。

Abstract: We derive the effective action governing the dynamics of a compact binary system when gravitational radiation is emitted by any mass or current multipole, scattered by the quasi-static field associated with the binary's angular momentum, and then reabsorbed. Among such angular momentum failed-tail processes, the ones involving multipole moments up to mass and current octupoles, which mix also with quadrupoles of opposite parity, contribute to the system dynamics at sixth post-Newtonian order; we display these terms explicitly as a particular case of our general derivation. Additionally, we derive the radiative multipole moments associated to arbitrary angular momentum failed-tails in emission processes.
